msg:Broadway Mansions stands out as an excellently situated hotel, conveniently near the Bund and iconic bridges, with Nanjing Road just 500 meters away ‚Äì an unbeatable location. However, communicating in English proves challenging for the staff, making it less expat-friendly, as it caters predominantly to a local clientele. The rooms impress with their spaciousness and preservation of classic items dating back to its inauguration in 1934. While the breakfast is satisfactory, there's room for enhancement, particularly in diversifying the fruit selection and paying more attention to detail. Despite these minor considerations, the hotel remains a compelling choice, offering great value compared to similar establishments in the area.

posted:Posted January 2, 2024
msg:Stayed at Shanghai Tower during the New Year. The hotel is located at Waibaidu Bridge and is very famous!
The surrounding environment of the hotel is first-class, including Pujiang Hotel, "Soviet Consulate", Waibaidu Bridge, South Suzhou River Road, Zhapu Road Bridge, Yuanmingyuan Road, etc. Of course, there are also the International Buildings on the Bund and the Lujiazui Four-piece Suite on the other side.
The hotel was built in 1934 and was known as "Broadway" at the time. The building's appearance is solemn and elegant, full of a sense of age!
The interior decoration of the hotel is grand. The small lobby is dotted with red objects, which is full of celebration. The long guest room corridor is full of mystery, which seems to tell you that this place was not something you could live in before.
The hotel buffet is rich in variety and the food tastes good. The long restaurant filled with Chinese and Western dishes and snacks demonstrates the five-star confidence.
The staff are enthusiastic, skillful and thoughtful, and they are very professional whether serving at the front desk, in the guest room or in the restaurant. Stayed for two nights and everything seemed fine.
However, there is still some regret.
The beautiful scenery outside the window of the guest room is endless, but the facilities in the room are a bit outdated: dim lights, cold toilet (you can't press it once to flush, you have to press it for a long time), and the incredible thing is the shower head. The water has almost no pressure and the water flow range is very small. These conditions are truly regrettable. At first glance, I thought, oh, this is an elderly society, and this "Broadway" is also old! just kidding.

    It was a surprise as soon as we checked in. Thanks to Manager Pan at the front desk, we were upgraded from a single room with river view to a suite room for five days for free. The view was even better (see the window view in the living room). A lot of the shooting equipment I brought could be used in the spacious room. Place and charge.
    The laptop I brought with me broke down the next day, and I had to ask the hotel's business depar**ent to provide a computer to help export a large amount of shooting data. Thank you to Manager Wang from the business depar**ent for the warm reception, providing a free desktop computer, and inviting the technical manager to help me analyze it. The reading and writing speed and other aspects are meticulous, which freed up space in the camera for my shooting the next day and saved time. The next day, a new laptop was delivered from Beijing to the hotel, and the handover at the front desk was very smooth.
    The manager of the restaurant on the top floor of Sanxie accompanied me to view the shooting angles outside the balcony of the restaurant during non-dining hours. Many of the angles were unique, and I raised my hand to take the photo.
    Shanghai Tower is the Shanghai Broadway Building in the 1930s, and the lobby is filled with period pictures and microcosms of historical events. Japanese-style fast food on the first floor, Yangzhou-style Chinese food on the second floor, private rooms and sightseeing balconies on the top floor, and songs and music by the old Shanghai singer Chen Gexin played in the hall (composed by his son Chen Gang&lt;Butterfly Lovers&gt;&gt;) , sliding door elevators with old Shanghai flavor on both sides, etc.
    The Zhapu Road Bridge downstairs is the check-in place for taking pictures of Pudong, and it is also the take-off and landing point for taking off drone shots in the morning and evening. Living in Shanghai Tower is connected in all directions, and the high-quality service of Shanghai Tower staff improves the daily efficiency of guests' visits and travels. Very complimentary. It will also be the best choice for staying in hotels in Shanghai in the future.

Shanghai Tower is strategically located at the confluence of Pujiang River and Suzhou Creek. First of all, from the hotel room, you can enjoy historical and modern buildings such as the Waibaidu Bridge on the Suzhou Creek, the Bund and buildings along the Pujiang River, the Oriental Pearl of Lujiazui, and the Jinmao Tower. posted:Posted January 29, 2023
msg:On the third day of the ***** New Year, I took the old man and the baby to live, and booked the Broadway Premier River View Suite in the nearly century-old landmark Shanghai Building. Premier Zhou received French President Pompidou, and he pointed out the Bund of the World Architecture Expo and Lujiazui, which was just a wasteland at that time, on the outdoor viewing platform on the 18th floor of the Shanghai Building.
My father had a special feeling for the Shanghai Building. It is said that when he was young, he rode a Phoenix bicycle to work here every day for 2 years. So when he heard that he finally had the opportunity to live here after decades, he was very excited.
This suite is not high, it is on the 7th floor, but it is on the west wing of the building (two wings), not only can you see the panoramic view of Pudong Lujiazui (see the sunrise from this angle), you can also see the Bund, Centennial Park Huangpu Park Monument to the People's Heroes, the Russian Consulate, the British Consulate on the Bund on the other side of the Suzhou River, the century-old Waibaidu Bridge downstairs, the confluence of one river and one river, even the master bedroom can clearly see the view of the Suzhou River to the west, the historical building Postal Building, etc. ( Key point: This angle can clearly see the magnificent sunset).
In the early morning, standing by the bed at sunrise, watching the skyline change from purple blue, gold, to pink blue, slowly dyeing the entire Shanghai Building and Waibaidu Bridge into an indescribable golden yellow
Sunset, from the west bed of the master bedroom, you can see a round of halo red sunset at the end of Suzhou Creek until it disappears at the end of the urban jungle.
The old man was very happy watching, especially the mother, who could only stand for 5 minutes due to physical reasons, and her mood improved a lot. He also pushed a wheelchair and took her to see the three treasures of the Shanghai Building‚Äîa century-old piano, a snooker table and scoreboard that are the same age as the building, and a hand-pulled elevator (unfortunately, only the floor pointer is left), and the elderly still watch it in the lobby There are so many photos of great people and celebrities, and it is very convenient to push a wheelchair from Huangpu Park to the Bund sightseeing wall at the door. The old mother even asked herself to walk for 5 minutes, and she was in a good mood looking at her condition.
The scenery is invincible, and the price/performance ratio is extremely high. The only place where you can see century-old Shanghai from three angles along the Huangpu River is the Shanghai Tower.
In addition, I was very impressed with Manager Huang in the hotel lobby. Due to the inconvenience of my mother's legs and feet, she has problems taking a bath. After all, it is a relatively old five-star hotel, and the facilities for the disabled cannot be perfected. Manager Huang not only provided a hotel wheelchair, but also provided us with reasonable suggestions. In the end, the old mother finished the bath smoothly.
In addition, the afternoon tea on the 14th floor was upgraded for us very well. It is very close to the place where Premier Zhou once stood. The old people are very happy üëèüëèüëè
Although the special requirements were a bit harsh, Manager Huang was very enthusiastic to solve the problems for the guests and satisfy the little wishes of the elderly. Thank you very much for this üôè! ! The service is very good! According to my habit, I really want to express my gratitude to the tip, but banknotes are not popular now, so it‚Äôs a pity that I don‚Äôt bring them with me üòÇüòÇ So I must praise this manager Huang (a gentleman who is fat and very lucky) )
What made a mistake this time was that I was busy taking pictures of the elderly and taking care of the baby, but I forgot to take pictures of this suite. I was really angry üò≠
The room is about 60 square meters! (In fact, I also booked a standard city-view room, which is also nearly 40 square meters), which is commendable for an old hotel with a history of nearly a hundred years!
The bed is moderately soft and hard, and the elderly have not complained about it being too soft to get up or having backaches. I like this!
The bathroom is full of marble countertops and huge mirrors, and the sense of space is still very good. The bathroom is separated from wet and dry. The kid insists on soaking in the bathtub, and it satisfies him. It‚Äôs quite funüíô
The layout of the corridor is exactly as I imagined. It needs to be turned around. It has the same meaning as the "Big Bird Cage" in Macau üòÅ I spent all my time on taking care of the elderly this time. Walk.

All the hotel guests showed up during breakfast, it was very lively, if you go early, you can sit by the landscape window and watch the scenery. There are quite a lot of things, and the dishes are quite satisfactory.
The dinner is also a Chinese set meal in the restaurant of the hotel. Everyone is full of praise for the lion head (it is said that it is a Huaiyang dish that Shanghai Mansion is good at)
Overall, it was a very good check-in experience. Manager Huang in the lobby added a lot of points to this stay üëçüëç
